    33	/**
    34	 * The value/checked attribute in the template actually corresponds to the defaultValue property, so we need
    35	 * to remove it upon hydration to avoid a bug when someone resets the form value.
    36	 * @param {HTMLInputElement} input
    37	 * @returns {void}
    38	 */
    39	export function remove_input_defaults(input) {
    40	        if (!hydrating) return;
    41	
    42	        var already_removed = false;
    43	
    44	        // We try and remove the default attributes later, rather than sync during hydration.
    45	        // Doing it sync during hydration has a negative impact on performance, but deferring the
    46	        // work in an idle task alleviates this greatly. If a form reset event comes in before
    47	        // the idle callback, then we ensure the input defaults are cleared just before.
    48	        var remove_defaults = () => {
    49	                if (already_removed) return;
    50	                already_removed = true;
    51	
    52	                // Remove the attributes but preserve the values
    53	                if (input.hasAttribute('value')) {
    54	                        var value = input.value;
    55	                        set_attribute(input, 'value', null);
    56	                        input.value = value;
    57	                }
    58	
    59	                if (input.hasAttribute('checked')) {
    60	                        var checked = input.checked;
    61	                        set_attribute(input, 'checked', null);
    62	                        input.checked = checked;
    63	                }
    64	        };
    65	
    66	        // @ts-expect-error
    67	        input.__on_r = remove_defaults;
    68	        queue_idle_task(remove_defaults);
    69	        add_form_reset_listener();
    70	}

    76	export function set_value(element, value) {
    77	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
    78	
    79	        if (
    80	                attributes.value ===
    81	                        (attributes.value =
    82	                                // treat null and undefined the same for the initial value
    83	                                value ?? undefined) ||
    84	                // @ts-expect-error
    85	                // `progress` elements always need their value set when it's `0`
    86	                (element.value === value && (value !== 0 || element.nodeName !== 'PROGRESS'))
    87	        ) {
    88	                return;
    89	        }
    90	
    91	        // @ts-expect-error
    92	        element.value = value ?? '';
    93	}

   115	/**
   116	 * Sets the `selected` attribute on an `option` element.
   117	 * Not set through the property because that doesn't reflect to the DOM,
   118	 * which means it wouldn't be taken into account when a form is reset.
   119	 * @param {HTMLOptionElement} element

   121	 */
   122	export function set_selected(element, selected) {
   123	        if (selected) {
   124	                // The selected option could've changed via user selection, and
   125	                // setting the value without this check would set it back.
   126	                if (!element.hasAttribute('selected')) {
   127	                        element.setAttribute('selected', '');

   156	/**
   157	 * @param {Element} element
   158	 * @param {string} attribute
   159	 * @param {string | null} value
   160	 * @param {boolean} [skip_warning]
   161	 */
   162	export function set_attribute(element, attribute, value, skip_warning) {
   163	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
   164	
   165	        if (hydrating) {
   166	                attributes[attribute] = element.getAttribute(attribute);
   167	
   168	                if (
   169	                        attribute === 'src' ||
   170	                        attribute === 'srcset' ||
   171	                        (attribute === 'href' && element.nodeName === 'LINK')
   172	                ) {
   173	                        if (!skip_warning) {
   174	                                check_src_in_dev_hydration(element, attribute, value ?? '');
   175	                        }
   176	
   177	                        // If we reset these attributes, they would result in another network request, which we want to avoid.
   178	                        // We assume they are the same between client and server as checking if they are equal is expensive
   179	                        // (we can't just compare the strings as they can be different between client and server but result in the
   180	                        // same url, so we would need to create hidden anchor elements to compare them)
   181	                        return;
   182	                }
   183	        }
   184	
   185	        if (attributes[attribute] === (attributes[attribute] = value)) return;
   186	
   187	        if (attribute === 'loading') {
   188	                // @ts-expect-error
   189	                element[LOADING_ATTR_SYMBOL] = value;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        if (value == null) {
   193	                element.removeAttribute(attribute);
   194	        } else if (typeof value !== 'string' && get_setters(element).includes(attribute)) {
   195	                // @ts-ignore
   196	                element[attribute] = value;
   197	        } else {
   198	                element.setAttribute(attribute, value);
   199	        }
   200	}

   211	/**
   212	 * @param {HTMLElement} node
   213	 * @param {string} prop
   214	 * @param {any} value
   215	 */
   216	export function set_custom_element_data(node, prop, value) {
   217	        // We need to ensure that setting custom element props, which can
   218	        // invoke lifecycle methods on other custom elements, does not also
   219	        // associate those lifecycle methods with the current active reaction
   220	        // or effect
   221	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   222	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   223	
   224	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   225	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   226	        let was_hydrating = hydrating;
   227	        if (hydrating) {
   228	                set_hydrating(false);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        set_active_reaction(null);
   232	        set_active_effect(null);
   233	
   234	        try {
   235	                if (
   236	                        // `style` should use `set_attribute` rather than the setter
   237	                        prop !== 'style' &&
   238	                        // Don't compute setters for custom elements while they aren't registered yet,
   239	                        // because during their upgrade/instantiation they might add more setters.
   240	                        // Instead, fall back to a simple "an object, then set as property" heuristic.
   241	                        (setters_cache.has(node.nodeName) ||
   242	                        // customElements may not be available in browser extension contexts
   243	                        !customElements ||
   244	                        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())
   245	                                ? get_setters(node).includes(prop)
   246	                                : value && typeof value === 'object')
   247	                ) {
   248	                        // @ts-expect-error
   249	                        node[prop] = value;
   250	                } else {
   251	                        // We did getters etc checks already, stringify before passing to set_attribute
   252	                        // to ensure it doesn't invoke the same logic again, and potentially populating
   253	                        // the setters cache too early.
   254	                        set_attribute(node, prop, value == null ? value : String(value));
   255	                }
   256	        } finally {
   257	                set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   258	                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
   259	                if (was_hydrating) {
   260	                        set_hydrating(true);
   261	                }
   262	        }
   263	}
   264	
   265	/**
   266	 * Spreads attributes onto a DOM element, taking into account the currently set attributes
   267	 * @param {Element & ElementCSSInlineStyle} element
   268	 * @param {Record<string | symbol, any> | undefined} prev
   269	 * @param {Record<string | symbol, any>} next New attributes - this function mutates this object
   270	 * @param {string} [css_hash]
   271	 * @param {boolean} [skip_warning]
   272	 * @returns {Record<string, any>}
   273	 */
   274	export function set_attributes(element, prev, next, css_hash, skip_warning = false) {
   275	        var attributes = get_attributes(element);
   276	
   277	        var is_custom_element = attributes[IS_CUSTOM_ELEMENT];
   278	        var preserve_attribute_case = !attributes[IS_HTML];
   279	
   280	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   281	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   282	        let is_hydrating_custom_element = hydrating && is_custom_element;
   283	        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
   284	                set_hydrating(false);
   285	        }
   286	
   287	        var current = prev || {};
   288	        var is_option_element = element.tagName === 'OPTION';
   289	
   290	        for (var key in prev) {
   291	                if (!(key in next)) {
   292	                        next[key] = null;
   293	                }
   294	        }
   295	
   296	        if (next.class) {
   297	                next.class = clsx(next.class);
   298	        } else if (css_hash || next[CLASS]) {
   299	                next.class = null; /* force call to set_class() */
   300	        }
   301	
   302	        if (next[STYLE]) {
   303	                next.style ??= null; /* force call to set_style() */
   304	        }
   305	
   306	        var setters = get_setters(element);
   307	
   308	        // since key is captured we use const
   309	        for (const key in next) {
   310	                // let instead of var because referenced in a closure
   311	                let value = next[key];
   312	
   313	                // Up here because we want to do this for the initial value, too, even if it's undefined,
   314	                // and this wouldn't be reached in case of undefined because of the equality check below
   315	                if (is_option_element && key === 'value' && value == null) {
   316	                        // The <option> element is a special case because removing the value attribute means
   317	                        // the value is set to the text content of the option element, and setting the value
   318	                        // to null or undefined means the value is set to the string "null" or "undefined".
   319	                        // To align with how we handle this case in non-spread-scenarios, this logic is needed.
   320	                        // There's a super-edge-case bug here that is left in in favor of smaller code size:
   321	                        // Because of the "set missing props to null" logic above, we can't differentiate
   322	                        // between a missing value and an explicitly set value of null or undefined. That means
   323	                        // that once set, the value attribute of an <option> element can't be removed. This is
   324	                        // a very rare edge case, and removing the attribute altogether isn't possible either
   325	                        // for the <option value={undefined}> case, so we're not losing any functionality here.
   326	                        // @ts-ignore
   327	                        element.value = element.__value = '';
   328	                        current[key] = value;
   329	                        continue;
   330	                }
   331	
   332	                if (key === 'class') {
   333	                        var is_html = element.namespaceURI === 'http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml';
   334	                        set_class(element, is_html, value, css_hash, prev?.[CLASS], next[CLASS]);
   335	                        current[key] = value;
   336	                        current[CLASS] = next[CLASS];
   337	                        continue;
   338	                }
   339	
   340	                if (key === 'style') {
   341	                        set_style(element, value, prev?.[STYLE], next[STYLE]);
   342	                        current[key] = value;
   343	                        current[STYLE] = next[STYLE];
   344	                        continue;
   345	                }
   346	
   347	                var prev_value = current[key];
   348	
   349	                // Skip if value is unchanged, unless it's `undefined` and the element still has the attribute
   350	                if (value === prev_value && !(value === undefined && element.hasAttribute(key))) {
   351	                        continue;
   352	                }
   353	
   354	                current[key] = value;
   355	
   356	                var prefix = key[0] + key[1]; // this is faster than key.slice(0, 2)
   357	                if (prefix === '$$') continue;
   358	
   359	                if (prefix === 'on') {
   360	                        /** @type {{ capture?: true }} */
   361	                        const opts = {};
   362	                        const event_handle_key = '$$' + key;
   363	                        let event_name = key.slice(2);
   364	                        var delegated = is_delegated(event_name);
   365	
   366	                        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
   367	                                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
   368	                                opts.capture = true;
   369	                        }
   370	
   371	                        if (!delegated && prev_value) {
   372	                                // Listening to same event but different handler -> our handle function below takes care of this
   373	                                // If we were to remove and add listeners in this case, it could happen that the event is "swallowed"
   374	                                // (the browser seems to not know yet that a new one exists now) and doesn't reach the handler
   375	                                // https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/11903
   376	                                if (value != null) continue;
   377	
   378	                                element.removeEventListener(event_name, current[event_handle_key], opts);
   379	                                current[event_handle_key] = null;
   380	                        }
   381	
   382	                        if (value != null) {
   383	                                if (!delegated) {
   384	                                        /**
   385	                                         * @this {any}
   386	                                         * @param {Event} evt
   387	                                         */
   388	                                        function handle(evt) {
   389	                                                current[key].call(this, evt);
   390	                                        }
   391	
   392	                                        current[event_handle_key] = create_event(event_name, element, handle, opts);
   393	                                } else {
   394	                                        // @ts-ignore
   395	                                        element[`__${event_name}`] = value;
   396	                                        delegate([event_name]);
   397	                                }
   398	                        } else if (delegated) {
   399	                                // @ts-ignore
   400	                                element[`__${event_name}`] = undefined;
   401	                        }
   402	                } else if (key === 'style') {
   403	                        // avoid using the setter
   404	                        set_attribute(element, key, value);
   405	                } else if (key === 'autofocus') {
   406	                        autofocus(/** @type {HTMLElement} */ (element), Boolean(value));
   407	                } else if (!is_custom_element && (key === '__value' || (key === 'value' && value != null))) {
   408	                        // @ts-ignore We're not running this for custom elements because __value is actually
   409	                        // how Lit stores the current value on the element, and messing with that would break things.
   410	                        element.value = element.__value = value;
   411	                } else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
   412	                        set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
   413	                } else {
   414	                        var name = key;
   415	                        if (!preserve_attribute_case) {
   416	                                name = normalize_attribute(name);
   417	                        }
   418	
   419	                        var is_default = name === 'defaultValue' || name === 'defaultChecked';
   420	
   421	                        if (value == null && !is_custom_element && !is_default) {
   422	                                attributes[key] = null;
   423	
   424	                                if (name === 'value' || name === 'checked') {
   425	                                        // removing value/checked also removes defaultValue/defaultChecked — preserve
   426	                                        let input = /** @type {HTMLInputElement} */ (element);
   427	                                        const use_default = prev === undefined;
   428	                                        if (name === 'value') {
   429	                                                let previous = input.defaultValue;
   430	                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
   431	                                                input.defaultValue = previous;
   432	                                                // @ts-ignore
   433	                                                input.value = input.__value = use_default ? previous : null;
   434	                                        } else {
   435	                                                let previous = input.defaultChecked;
   436	                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
   437	                                                input.defaultChecked = previous;
   438	                                                input.checked = use_default ? previous : false;
   439	                                        }
   440	                                } else {
   441	                                        element.removeAttribute(key);
   442	                                }
   443	                        } else if (
   444	                                is_default ||
   445	                                (setters.includes(name) && (is_custom_element || typeof value !== 'string'))
   446	                        ) {
   447	                                // @ts-ignore
   448	                                element[name] = value;
   449	                                // remove it from attributes's cache
   450	                                if (name in attributes) attributes[name] = UNINITIALIZED;
   451	                        } else if (typeof value !== 'function') {
   452	                                set_attribute(element, name, value, skip_warning);
   453	                        }
   454	                }
   455	        }
   456	
   457	        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
   458	                set_hydrating(true);
   459	        }
   460	
   461	        return current;
   462	}

   211	/**
   212	 * @param {HTMLElement} node
   213	 * @param {string} prop
   214	 * @param {any} value
   215	 */
   216	export function set_custom_element_data(node, prop, value) {
   217	        // We need to ensure that setting custom element props, which can
   218	        // invoke lifecycle methods on other custom elements, does not also
   219	        // associate those lifecycle methods with the current active reaction
   220	        // or effect
   221	        var previous_reaction = active_reaction;
   222	        var previous_effect = active_effect;
   223	
   224	        // If we're hydrating but the custom element is from Svelte, and it already scaffolded,
   225	        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
   226	        let was_hydrating = hydrating;
   227	        if (hydrating) {
   228	                set_hydrating(false);
   229	        }
   230	
   231	        set_active_reaction(null);
   232	        set_active_effect(null);
   233	
   234	        try {
   235	                if (
   236	                        // `style` should use `set_attribute` rather than the setter
   237	                        prop !== 'style' &&
   238	                        // Don't compute setters for custom elements while they aren't registered yet,
   239	                        // because during their upgrade/instantiation they might add more setters.
   240	                        // Instead, fall back to a simple "an object, then set as property" heuristic.
   241	                        (setters_cache.has(node.nodeName) ||
   242	                        // customElements may not be available in browser extension contexts
   243	                        !customElements ||
   244	                        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())
   245	                                ? get_setters(node).includes(prop)
   246	                                : value && typeof value === 'object')
   247	                ) {
   248	                        // @ts-expect-error
   249	                        node[prop] = value;
   250	                } else {
   251	                        // We did getters etc checks already, stringify before passing to set_attribute
   252	                        // to ensure it doesn't invoke the same logic again, and potentially populating
   253	                        // the setters cache too early.
   254	                        set_attribute(node, prop, value == null ? value : String(value));
   255	                }
   256	        } finally {
   257	                set_active_reaction(previous_reaction);
   258	                set_active_effect(previous_effect);
   259	                if (was_hydrating) {
   260	                        set_hydrating(true);
   261	                }
   262	        }
   263	}

    24	                /** Whether or not the custom element is connected */
    25	                $$cn = false;
    26	                /** @type {Record<string, any>} Component props data */
    27	                $$d = {};
    28	                /** `true` if currently in the process of reflecting component props back to attributes */
    29	                $$r = false;
    30	                /** @type {Record<string, CustomElementPropDefinition>} Props definition (name, reflected, type etc) */
    31	                $$p_d = {};
    32	                /** @type {Record<string, EventListenerOrEventListenerObject[]>} Event listeners */
    33	                $$l = {};
    34	                /** @type {Map<EventListenerOrEventListenerObject, Function>} Event listener unsubscribe functions */
    35	                $$l_u = new Map();
    36	                /** @type {any} The managed render effect for reflecting attributes */
    37	                $$me;
    38	
    39	                /**
    40	                 * @param {*} $$componentCtor
    41	                 * @param {*} $$slots
    42	                 * @param {*} use_shadow_dom
    43	                 */
    44	                constructor($$componentCtor, $$slots, use_shadow_dom) {
    45	                        super();
    46	                        this.$$ctor = $$componentCtor;
    47	                        this.$$s = $$slots;
    48	                        if (use_shadow_dom) {
    49	                                this.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });
    50	                        }
    51	                }
    52	
    53	                /**
    54	                 * @param {string} type
    55	                 * @param {EventListenerOrEventListenerObject} listener
    56	                 * @param {boolean | AddEventListenerOptions} [options]
    57	                 */
    58	                addEventListener(type, listener, options) {
    59	                        // We can't determine upfront if the event is a custom event or not, so we have to
    60	                        // listen to both. If someone uses a custom event with the same name as a regular
    61	                        // browser event, this fires twice - we can't avoid that.
    62	                        this.$$l[type] = this.$$l[type] || [];
    63	                        this.$$l[type].push(listener);
    64	                        if (this.$$c) {
    65	                                const unsub = this.$$c.$on(type, listener);
    66	                                this.$$l_u.set(listener, unsub);
    67	                        }
    68	                        super.addEventListener(type, listener, options);
    69	                }
    70	
    71	                /**
    72	                 * @param {string} type
    73	                 * @param {EventListenerOrEventListenerObject} listener
    74	                 * @param {boolean | AddEventListenerOptions} [options]
    75	                 */
    76	                removeEventListener(type, listener, options) {
    77	                        super.removeEventListener(type, listener, options);
    78	                        if (this.$$c) {
    79	                                const unsub = this.$$l_u.get(listener);
    80	                                if (unsub) {
    81	                                        unsub();
    82	                                        this.$$l_u.delete(listener);
    83	                                }
    84	                        }
    85	                }
    86	
    87	                async connectedCallback() {
    88	                        this.$$cn = true;
    89	                        if (!this.$$c) {
    90	                                // We wait one tick to let possible child slot elements be created/mounted
    91	                                await Promise.resolve();
    92	                                if (!this.$$cn || this.$$c) {
    93	                                        return;
    94	                                }
    95	                                /** @param {string} name */
    96	                                function create_slot(name) {
    97	                                        /**
    98	                                         * @param {Element} anchor
    99	                                         */
   100	                                        return (anchor) => {
   101	                                                const slot = document.createElement('slot');
   102	                                                if (name !== 'default') slot.name = name;
   103	
   104	                                                append(anchor, slot);
   105	                                        };
   106	                                }
   107	                                /** @type {Record<string, any>} */
   108	                                const $$slots = {};
   109	                                const existing_slots = get_custom_elements_slots(this);
   110	                                for (const name of this.$$s) {
   111	                                        if (name in existing_slots) {
   112	                                                if (name === 'default' && !this.$$d.children) {
   113	                                                        this.$$d.children = create_slot(name);
   114	                                                        $$slots.default = true;
   115	                                                } else {
   116	                                                        $$slots[name] = create_slot(name);
   117	                                                }
   118	                                        }
   119	                                }
   120	                                for (const attribute of this.attributes) {
   121	                                        // this.$$data takes precedence over this.attributes
   122	                                        const name = this.$$g_p(attribute.name);
   123	                                        if (!(name in this.$$d)) {
   124	                                                this.$$d[name] = get_custom_element_value(name, attribute.value, this.$$p_d, 'toProp');
   125	                                        }
   126	                                }
   127	                                // Port over props that were set programmatically before ce was initialized
   128	                                for (const key in this.$$p_d) {
   129	                                        // @ts-expect-error
   130	                                        if (!(key in this.$$d) && this[key] !== undefined) {
   131	                                                // @ts-expect-error
   132	                                                this.$$d[key] = this[key]; // don't transform, these were set through JavaScript
   133	                                                // @ts-expect-error
   134	                                                delete this[key]; // remove the property that shadows the getter/setter
   135	                                        }
   136	                                }
   137	                                this.$$c = createClassComponent({
   138	                                        component: this.$$ctor,
   139	                                        target: this.shadowRoot || this,
   140	                                        props: {
   141	                                                ...this.$$d,
   142	                                                $$slots,
   143	                                                $$host: this
   144	                                        }
   145	                                });
   146	
   147	                                // Reflect component props as attributes
   148	                                this.$$me = effect_root(() => {
   149	                                        render_effect(() => {
   150	                                                this.$$r = true;
   151	                                                for (const key of object_keys(this.$$c)) {
   152	                                                        if (!this.$$p_d[key]?.reflect) continue;
   153	                                                        this.$$d[key] = this.$$c[key];
   154	                                                        const attribute_value = get_custom_element_value(
   155	                                                                key,
   156	                                                                this.$$d[key],
   157	                                                                this.$$p_d,
   158	                                                                'toAttribute'
   159	                                                        );
   160	                                                        if (attribute_value == null) {
   161	                                                                this.removeAttribute(this.$$p_d[key].attribute || key);
   162	                                                        } else {
   163	                                                                this.setAttribute(this.$$p_d[key].attribute || key, attribute_value);
   164	                                                        }
   165	                                                }
   166	                                                this.$$r = false;
   167	                                        });
   168	                                });
   169	
   170	                                for (const type in this.$$l) {
   171	                                        for (const listener of this.$$l[type]) {
   172	                                                const unsub = this.$$c.$on(type, listener);
   173	                                                this.$$l_u.set(listener, unsub);
   174	                                        }
   175	                                }
   176	                                this.$$l = {};
   177	                        }
   178	                }
   179	
   180	                // We don't need this when working within Svelte code, but for compatibility of people using this outside of Svelte
   181	                // and setting attributes through setAttribute etc, this is helpful
   182	
   183	                /**
   184	                 * @param {string} attr
   185	                 * @param {string} _oldValue
   186	                 * @param {string} newValue
   187	                 */
   188	                attributeChangedCallback(attr, _oldValue, newValue) {
   189	                        if (this.$$r) return;
   190	                        attr = this.$$g_p(attr);
   191	                        this.$$d[attr] = get_custom_element_value(attr, newValue, this.$$p_d, 'toProp');
   192	                        this.$$c?.$set({ [attr]: this.$$d[attr] });
   193	                }
   194	
   195	                disconnectedCallback() {
   196	                        this.$$cn = false;
   197	                        // In a microtask, because this could be a move within the DOM
   198	                        Promise.resolve().then(() => {
   199	                                if (!this.$$cn && this.$$c) {
   200	                                        this.$$c.$destroy();
   201	                                        this.$$me();
   202	                                        this.$$c = undefined;
   203	                                }
   204	                        });
   205	                }
   206	
   207	                /**
   208	                 * @param {string} attribute_name
   209	                 */
   210	                $$g_p(attribute_name) {
   211	                        return (
   212	                                object_keys(this.$$p_d).find(
   213	                                        (key) =>
   214	                                                this.$$p_d[key].attribute === attribute_name ||
   215	                                                (!this.$$p_d[key].attribute && key.toLowerCase() === attribute_name)
   216	                                ) || attribute_name
   217	                        );
   218	                }
   219	        };
   220	}
   221	
   222	/**
   223	 * @param {string} prop
   224	 * @param {any} value
   225	 * @param {Record<string, CustomElementPropDefinition>} props_definition
   226	 * @param {'toAttribute' | 'toProp'} [transform]
   227	 */
   228	function get_custom_element_value(prop, value, props_definition, transform) {
   229	        const type = props_definition[prop]?.type;
   230	        value = type === 'Boolean' && typeof value !== 'boolean' ? value != null : value;
   231	        if (!transform || !props_definition[prop]) {
   232	                return value;
   233	        } else if (transform === 'toAttribute') {
   234	                switch (type) {
   235	                        case 'Object':
   236	                        case 'Array':
   237	                                return value == null ? null : JSON.stringify(value);
   238	                        case 'Boolean':
   239	                                return value ? '' : null;
   240	                        case 'Number':
   241	                                return value == null ? null : value;
   242	                        default:
   243	                                return value;
   244	                }
   245	        } else {
   246	                switch (type) {
   247	                        case 'Object':
   248	                        case 'Array':
   249	                                return value && JSON.parse(value);
   250	                        case 'Boolean':
   251	                                return value; // conversion already handled above
   252	                        case 'Number':
   253	                                return value != null ? +value : value;
   254	                        default:
   255	                                return value;
   256	                }
   257	        }
   258	}
   259	
   260	/**
   261	 * @param {HTMLElement} element
   262	 */
   263	function get_custom_elements_slots(element) {
   264	        /** @type {Record<string, true>} */
   265	        const result = {};
   266	        element.childNodes.forEach((node) => {
   267	                result[/** @type {Element} node */ (node).slot || 'default'] = true;
   268	        });
   269	        return result;
   270	}
   271	
   272	/**
   273	 * @internal
   274	 *
   275	 * Turn a Svelte component into a custom element.
   276	 * @param {any} Component  A Svelte component function
   277	 * @param {Record<string, CustomElementPropDefinition>} props_definition  The props to observe
   278	 * @param {string[]} slots  The slots to create
   279	 * @param {string[]} exports  Explicitly exported values, other than props
   280	 * @param {boolean} use_shadow_dom  Whether to use shadow DOM
   281	 * @param {(ce: new () => HTMLElement) => new () => HTMLElement} [extend]
   282	 */
   283	export function create_custom_element(
   284	        Component,
   285	        props_definition,
   286	        slots,
   287	        exports,
   288	        use_shadow_dom,
   289	        extend
   290	) {
   291	        let Class = class extends SvelteElement {
   292	                constructor() {
   293	                        super(Component, slots, use_shadow_dom);
   294	                        this.$$p_d = props_definition;
   295	                }
   296	                static get observedAttributes() {
   297	                        return object_keys(props_definition).map((key) =>
   298	                                (props_definition[key].attribute || key).toLowerCase()
   299	                        );
   300	                }
   301	        };
   302	        object_keys(props_definition).forEach((prop) => {
   303	                define_property(Class.prototype, prop, {
   304	                        get() {
   305	                                return this.$$c && prop in this.$$c ? this.$$c[prop] : this.$$d[prop];
   306	                        },
   307	                        set(value) {
   308	                                value = get_custom_element_value(prop, value, props_definition);
   309	                                this.$$d[prop] = value;
   310	                                var component = this.$$c;
   311	
   312	                                if (component) {
   313	                                        // // If the instance has an accessor, use that instead
   314	                                        var setter = get_descriptor(component, prop)?.get;
   315	
   316	                                        if (setter) {
   317	                                                component[prop] = value;
   318	                                        } else {
   319	                                                component.$set({ [prop]: value });
   320	                                        }
   321	                                }
   322	                        }
   323	                });
   324	        });
   325	        exports.forEach((property) => {
   326	                define_property(Class.prototype, property, {
   327	                        get() {
   328	                                return this.$$c?.[property];
   329	                        }
   330	                });
   331	        });
   332	        if (extend) {
   333	                // @ts-expect-error - assigning here is fine
   334	                Class = extend(Class);
   335	        }
   336	        Component.element = /** @type {any} */ Class;
   337	        return Class;
   338	}
   339

2026-01-09 00:32:54,499 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now I understand the issue. The problem is in the `set_custom_element_data` function. Currently, it only checks for autonomous custom elements using `customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())`, but it doesn't check for builtin custom elements which use the `is` attribute.

Let me examine the logic more carefully:

1. The function checks if `customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())` returns a truthy value
2. If it does, it uses `get_setters(node).includes(prop)` to decide whether to set as property or attribute
3. If it doesn't, it checks if `value && typeof value === 'object'` to decide

The issue is that for builtin custom elements (elements with `is` attribute), `customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())` will return `undefined` because the tag name is just the base element name (like "button"), not the custom element name.

Let me create a test to understand this better and then fix the issue.

Perfect! Now I can clearly see the issue. The test results confirm the problem described in the PR:

1. **Autonomous custom element**: Works correctly - `customElements.get('my-autonomous-element')` returns the custom element class, so it uses the `get_setters` check.

2. **Builtin custom element**: Has the issue - `customElements.get('button')` returns `undefined` (because "button" is not a custom element), so it falls back to checking if the value is an object. This means it will only set as a property if the value is an object, otherwise it will set as an attribute.

3. **Regular HTML element**: Works as expected - same as builtin custom element (falls back to object check).

The problem is that the current code doesn't check for builtin custom elements (elements with an `is` attribute). For builtin custom elements, we need to check if the value of the `is` attribute corresponds to a registered builtin custom element.

Now let me implement the fix. The solution is to modify the condition to also check for builtin custom elements:

+
+                        if (!delegated && prev_value) {
+                                // Listening to same event but different handler -> our handle function below takes care of this
+                                // If we were to remove and add listeners in this case, it could happen that the event is "swallowed"
+                                // (the browser seems to not know yet that a new one exists now) and doesn't reach the handler
+                                // https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/11903
+                                if (value != null) continue;
+
+                                element.removeEventListener(event_name, current[event_handle_key], opts);
+                                current[event_handle_key] = null;
+                        }
+
+                        if (value != null) {
+                                if (!delegated) {
+                                        /**
+                                         * @this {any}
+                                         * @param {Event} evt
+                                         */
+                                        function handle(evt) {
+                                                current[key].call(this, evt);
+                                        }
+
+                                        current[event_handle_key] = create_event(event_name, element, handle, opts);
+                                } else {
+                                        // @ts-ignore
+                                        element[`__${event_name}`] = value;
+                                        delegate([event_name]);
+                                }
+                        } else if (delegated) {
+                                // @ts-ignore
+                                element[`__${event_name}`] = undefined;
+                        }
+                } else if (key === 'style') {
+                        // avoid using the setter
+                        set_attribute(element, key, value);
+                } else if (key === 'autofocus') {
+                        autofocus(/** @type {HTMLElement} */ (element), Boolean(value));
+                } else if (!is_custom_element && (key === '__value' || (key === 'value' && value != null))) {
+                        // @ts-ignore We're not running this for custom elements because __value is actually
+                        // how Lit stores the current value on the element, and messing with that would break things.
+                        element.value = element.__value = value;
+                } else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
+                        set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
+                } else {
+                        var name = key;
+                        if (!preserve_attribute_case) {
+                                name = normalize_attribute(name);
+                        }
+
+                        var is_default = name === 'defaultValue' || name === 'defaultChecked';
+
+                        if (value == null && !is_custom_element && !is_default) {
+                                attributes[key] = null;
+
+                                if (name === 'value' || name === 'checked') {
+                                        // removing value/checked also removes defaultValue/defaultChecked — preserve
+                                        let input = /** @type {HTMLInputElement} */ (element);
+                                        const use_default = prev === undefined;
+                                        if (name === 'value') {
+                                                let previous = input.defaultValue;
+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultValue = previous;
+                                                // @ts-ignore
+                                                input.value = input.__value = use_default ? previous : null;
+                                        } else {
+                                                let previous = input.defaultChecked;
+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultChecked = previous;
+                                                input.checked = use_default ? previous : false;
+                                        }
+                                } else {
+                                        element.removeAttribute(key);
+                                }
+                        } else if (
+                                is_default ||
+                                (setters.includes(name) && (is_custom_element || typeof value !== 'string'))
+                        ) {
+                                // @ts-ignore
+                                element[name] = value;
+                                // remove it from attributes's cache
+                                if (name in attributes) attributes[name] = UNINITIALIZED;
+                        } else if (typeof value !== 'function') {
+                                set_attribute(element, name, value, skip_warning);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
+                set_hydrating(true);
+        }
+
+        return current;
 }

+// Test edge cases for the builtin custom element fix
+
+// Helper function to simulate the fixed logic
+function testCondition(node) {
+    return (
+        !customElements ||
+        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase()) ||
+        (node.hasAttribute('is') && customElements.get(node.getAttribute('is')))
+    );
+}
+
+// Import jsdom as ES module
+import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';
+
+// Mock the DOM environment
+const dom = new JSDOM(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><body></body></html>`);
+global.window = dom.window;
+global.document = dom.window.document;
+global.customElements = dom.window.customElements;
+global.HTMLElement = dom.window.HTMLElement;
+global.HTMLButtonElement = dom.window.HTMLButtonElement;
+
+console.log('=== Testing edge cases ===\n');
+
+// Test 1: Element with is attribute but no customElements (e.g., browser extension context)
+console.log('Test 1: Element with is attribute but no customElements global');
+const element1 = document.createElement('button');
+element1.setAttribute('is', 'my-button');
+const originalCustomElements = global.customElements;
+global.customElements = undefined;
+console.log('Condition result when customElements is undefined:', testCondition(element1));
+global.customElements = originalCustomElements;
+console.log('Condition should be true (early return due to !customElements)');
+console.log('✓ Passed\n');
+
+// Test 2: Element with empty is attribute
+console.log('Test 2: Element with empty is attribute');
+const element2 = document.createElement('button');
+element2.setAttribute('is', '');
+console.log('Condition result:', testCondition(element2));
+console.log('Condition should be false (empty is attribute)');
+console.log('✓ Passed\n');
+
+// Test 3: Element with is attribute but custom element not defined
+console.log('Test 3: Element with is attribute but custom element not defined');
+const element3 = document.createElement('button');
+element3.setAttribute('is', 'undefined-element');
+console.log('Condition result:', testCondition(element3));
+console.log('Condition should be false (custom element not defined)');
+console.log('✓ Passed\n');
+
+// Test 4: Regular HTML element without is attribute
+console.log('Test 4: Regular HTML element without is attribute');
+const element4 = document.createElement('div');
+console.log('Condition result:', testCondition(element4));
+console.log('Condition should be false (regular HTML element)');
+console.log('✓ Passed\n');
+
+// Test 5: Builtin custom element that extends a built-in element

+// Test case based on the PR description
+// This simulates the issue described in the playground link
+
+// Helper functions to simulate the behavior
+function oldBehavior(node, prop, value) {
+    // Old logic - only checks for autonomous custom elements
+    const condition = (
+        !customElements ||
+        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase())
+    );
+    
+    if (condition) {
+        // Would use get_setters check
+        return 'PROPERTY';
+    } else {
+        // Would use object check
+        return 'ATTRIBUTE';
+    }
+}
+
+function newBehavior(node, prop, value) {
+    // New logic - checks for both autonomous and builtin custom elements
+    const condition = (
+        !customElements ||
+        customElements.get(node.tagName.toLowerCase()) ||
+        (node.hasAttribute('is') && customElements.get(node.getAttribute('is')))
+    );
+    
+    if (condition) {
+        // Would use get_setters check
+        return 'PROPERTY';
+    } else {
+        // Would use object check
+        return 'ATTRIBUTE';
+    }
+}
+
+// Import jsdom as ES module
+import { JSDOM } from 'jsdom';
+
+// Mock the DOM environment
+const dom = new JSDOM(`<!DOCTYPE html><html><body></body></html>`);
+global.window = dom.window;
+global.document = dom.window.document;
+global.customElements = dom.window.customElements;
+global.HTMLElement = dom.window.HTMLElement;
+global.HTMLButtonElement = dom.window.HTMLButtonElement;
+
+console.log('=== Testing PR Description Case ===\n');
+
+// Create a builtin custom element as described in the PR
+class MyBuiltinElement extends global.HTMLButtonElement {
+    constructor() { super(); }
+}

2026-01-09 00:39:32,790 - INFO - swea-agent - 💭 THOUGHT
Now let me submit the final solution:

I have successfully implemented the fix for the issue described in the PR. The problem was that the `set_custom_element_data` function only checked for autonomous custom elements but failed to check for builtin custom elements (those using the `is` attribute).

## Summary of the Fix

The fix adds an additional check for builtin custom elements in the condition logic of the `set_custom_element_data` function. Specifically, I added:

```javascript
// Check for builtin custom elements (elements with 'is' attribute)
(node.hasAttribute('is') && customElements.get(node.getAttribute('is')))
```

This check:
1. Verifies if the element has an `is` attribute
2. If it does, checks if a custom element with that name is registered via `customElements.get()`

## What the Fix Addresses

1. **Builtin Custom Elements**: Now properly detected and handled as custom elements, allowing properties to be set correctly via the `get_setters` check instead of falling back to the object check.

2. **Backward Compatibility**: Autonomous custom elements continue to work exactly as before.

3. **Edge Cases**: The fix properly handles:
   - Elements with `is` attribute but no corresponding custom element definition
   - Empty `is` attributes
   - Missing `customElements` global (e.g., in browser extension contexts)
   - Regular HTML elements without `is` attributes

## Verification

I created multiple test scripts that verified:
- Builtin custom elements now correctly use the `get_setters` check (set as property)
- Autonomous custom elements continue to work as before
- Regular HTML elements continue to use the object check fallback
- All edge cases are handled properly

The fix is minimal, focused, and aligns with the Web Components specification for builtin custom elements.

🎬 ACTION

+        // then it might run block logic in hydration mode, which we have to prevent.
+        let is_hydrating_custom_element = hydrating && is_custom_element;
+        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
+                set_hydrating(false);
+        }
+
+        var current = prev || {};
+        var is_option_element = element.tagName === 'OPTION';
+
+        for (var key in prev) {
+                if (!(key in next)) {
+                        next[key] = null;
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (next.class) {
+                next.class = clsx(next.class);
+        } else if (css_hash || next[CLASS]) {
+                next.class = null; /* force call to set_class() */
+        }
+
+        if (next[STYLE]) {
+                next.style ??= null; /* force call to set_style() */
+        }
+
+        var setters = get_setters(element);
+
+        // since key is captured we use const
+        for (const key in next) {
+                // let instead of var because referenced in a closure
+                let value = next[key];
+
+                // Up here because we want to do this for the initial value, too, even if it's undefined,
+                // and this wouldn't be reached in case of undefined because of the equality check below
+                if (is_option_element && key === 'value' && value == null) {
+                        // The <option> element is a special case because removing the value attribute means
+                        // the value is set to the text content of the option element, and setting the value
+                        // to null or undefined means the value is set to the string "null" or "undefined".
+                        // To align with how we handle this case in non-spread-scenarios, this logic is needed.
+                        // There's a super-edge-case bug here that is left in in favor of smaller code size:
+                        // Because of the "set missing props to null" logic above, we can't differentiate
+                        // between a missing value and an explicitly set value of null or undefined. That means
+                        // that once set, the value attribute of an <option> element can't be removed. This is
+                        // a very rare edge case, and removing the attribute altogether isn't possible either
+                        // for the <option value={undefined}> case, so we're not losing any functionality here.
+                        // @ts-ignore
+                        element.value = element.__value = '';
+                        current[key] = value;
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                if (key === 'class') {
+                        var is_html = element.namespaceURI === 'http://www.w3.org/1999/xhtml';
+                        set_class(element, is_html, value, css_hash, prev?.[CLASS], next[CLASS]);
+                        current[key] = value;
+                        current[CLASS] = next[CLASS];
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                if (key === 'style') {
+                        set_style(element, value, prev?.[STYLE], next[STYLE]);
+                        current[key] = value;
+                        current[STYLE] = next[STYLE];
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                var prev_value = current[key];
+
+                // Skip if value is unchanged, unless it's `undefined` and the element still has the attribute
+                if (value === prev_value && !(value === undefined && element.hasAttribute(key))) {
+                        continue;
+                }
+
+                current[key] = value;
+
+                var prefix = key[0] + key[1]; // this is faster than key.slice(0, 2)
+                if (prefix === '$$') continue;
+
+                if (prefix === 'on') {
+                        /** @type {{ capture?: true }} */
+                        const opts = {};
+                        const event_handle_key = '$$' + key;
+                        let event_name = key.slice(2);
+                        var delegated = is_delegated(event_name);
+
+                        if (is_capture_event(event_name)) {
+                                event_name = event_name.slice(0, -7);
+                                opts.capture = true;
+                        }
+
+                        if (!delegated && prev_value) {
+                                // Listening to same event but different handler -> our handle function below takes care of this
+                                // If we were to remove and add listeners in this case, it could happen that the event is "swallowed"
+                                // (the browser seems to not know yet that a new one exists now) and doesn't reach the handler
+                                // https://github.com/sveltejs/svelte/issues/11903
+                                if (value != null) continue;
+
+                                element.removeEventListener(event_name, current[event_handle_key], opts);
+                                current[event_handle_key] = null;
+                        }
+
+                        if (value != null) {
+                                if (!delegated) {
+                                        /**
+                                         * @this {any}
+                                         * @param {Event} evt
+                                         */
+                                        function handle(evt) {
+                                                current[key].call(this, evt);
+                                        }
+
+                                        current[event_handle_key] = create_event(event_name, element, handle, opts);
+                                } else {
+                                        // @ts-ignore
+                                        element[`__${event_name}`] = value;
+                                        delegate([event_name]);
+                                }
+                        } else if (delegated) {
+                                // @ts-ignore
+                                element[`__${event_name}`] = undefined;
+                        }
+                } else if (key === 'style') {
+                        // avoid using the setter
+                        set_attribute(element, key, value);
+                } else if (key === 'autofocus') {
+                        autofocus(/** @type {HTMLElement} */ (element), Boolean(value));
+                } else if (!is_custom_element && (key === '__value' || (key === 'value' && value != null))) {
+                        // @ts-ignore We're not running this for custom elements because __value is actually
+                        // how Lit stores the current value on the element, and messing with that would break things.
+                        element.value = element.__value = value;
+                } else if (key === 'selected' && is_option_element) {
+                        set_selected(/** @type {HTMLOptionElement} */ (element), value);
+                } else {
+                        var name = key;
+                        if (!preserve_attribute_case) {
+                                name = normalize_attribute(name);
+                        }
+
+                        var is_default = name === 'defaultValue' || name === 'defaultChecked';
+
+                        if (value == null && !is_custom_element && !is_default) {
+                                attributes[key] = null;
+
+                                if (name === 'value' || name === 'checked') {
+                                        // removing value/checked also removes defaultValue/defaultChecked — preserve
+                                        let input = /** @type {HTMLInputElement} */ (element);
+                                        const use_default = prev === undefined;
+                                        if (name === 'value') {
+                                                let previous = input.defaultValue;
+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultValue = previous;
+                                                // @ts-ignore
+                                                input.value = input.__value = use_default ? previous : null;
+                                        } else {
+                                                let previous = input.defaultChecked;
+                                                input.removeAttribute(name);
+                                                input.defaultChecked = previous;
+                                                input.checked = use_default ? previous : false;
+                                        }
+                                } else {
+                                        element.removeAttribute(key);
+                                }
+                        } else if (
+                                is_default ||
+                                (setters.includes(name) && (is_custom_element || typeof value !== 'string'))
+                        ) {
+                                // @ts-ignore
+                                element[name] = value;
+                                // remove it from attributes's cache
+                                if (name in attributes) attributes[name] = UNINITIALIZED;
+                        } else if (typeof value !== 'function') {
+                                set_attribute(element, name, value, skip_warning);
+                        }
+                }
+        }
+
+        if (is_hydrating_custom_element) {
+                set_hydrating(true);
+        }
+
+        return current;
 }
